# NUMERIC CFO MEGA TRAINING SUITE

Enterprise Ecommerce / Retail / Wholesale Finance Numeric Training
Dataset

Contains: - Numeric financial statement scenarios - EBITDA / Cash /
Contribution calculations - Inventory planning math problems - Pricing
and CAC decision cases - Spreadsheet-style dependency tracing

All cases include structured numeric inputs suitable for evaluation
datasets.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
